<t>CREATE TABLE Cars (car_id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_make VARCHAR(50), car_model VARCHAR(50), year INT, color VARCHAR(20))

CREATE TABLE Owners (owner_id INT PRIMARY KEY, owner_name VARCHAR(50), contact_number VARCHAR(15))

CREATE TABLE Services (service_id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES Cars(car_id), service_type VARCHAR(50), date DATE, cost DECIMAL(10,2))

CREATE TABLE Parts (part_id INT PRIMARY KEY, part_name VARCHAR(50), quantity INT, cost DECIMAL(10,2))</t><s>UPSERT INTO Cars (car_id, car_make, car_model, year, color) VALUES (1, 'Toyota', 'Camry', 2021, 'Red') ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE car_make='Toyota', car_model='Camry', year=2021, color='Red'</s>

<t>CREATE TABLE car(id INT PRIMARY KEY, brand VARCHAR(50), model VARCHAR(50))

CREATE TABLE engine(id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES car(id), type VARCHAR(50), hp INT)

CREATE TABLE chassis(id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES car(id), material VARCHAR(50), color VARCHAR(50))

CREATE TABLE tire(id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES car(id), brand VARCHAR(50), size VARCHAR(10), type VARCHAR(50))

CREATE TABLE maintenance(id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES car(id), type VARCHAR(50), date DATE)</t><s>INSERT INTO car (id, brand, model) VALUES (1, 'Toyota', 'Corolla') ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET brand = excluded.brand, model = excluded.model</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE car(id INT PRIMARY KEY, brand VARCHAR(50), model VARCHAR(50))

CREATE TABLE tire(id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES car(id), brand VARCHAR(50), size VARCHAR(10), type VARCHAR(50))</t><s>INSERT INTO car (id, brand, model) VALUES (1, 'Toyota', 'Corolla') ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET brand = excluded.brand, model = excluded.model</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE engine(id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES car(id), type VARCHAR(50), hp INT)

CREATE TABLE engine(id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES car(id), type VARCHAR(50), hp INT)</t><s>INSERT INTO car (id, brand, model) VALUES (1, 'Toyota', 'Corolla') ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET brand = excluded.brand, model = excluded.model</s>

CREATE TABLE engine(id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES car(id), type VARCHAR(50), hp INT)</t><s>INSERT INTO car (id, brand, model) VALUES (1, 'Toyota', 'Corolla') ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET brand = excluded.brand, model = excluded.model</s>

CREATE TABLE tire(id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES car(id), brand VARCHAR(50), size VARCHAR(10), type VARCHAR(50))

CREATE TABLE maintenance(id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES car(id), type VARCHAR(50), date DATE)

CREATE TABLE car(id INT PRIMARY KEY, brand VARCHAR(50), model VARCHAR(50))</t><s>insert into engine (id, car_id, type, hp) values (1, 1, 'v8', 400) on conflict (id) do update set car_id = excluded.car_id, type = excluded.type, hp = excluded.hp</s>

CREATE TABLE car(id INT PRIMARY KEY, brand VARCHAR(50), model VARCHAR(50))

<t>CREATE TABLE car(id INT PRIMARY KEY, brand VARCHAR(50), model VARCHAR(50))

CREATE TABLE chassis(id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES car(id), material VARCHAR(50), color VARCHAR(50))

CREATE TABLE maintenance(id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES car(id), type VARCHAR(50), date DATE)

CREATE TABLE tire(id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES car(id), brand VARCHAR(50), size VARCHAR(10), type VARCHAR(50))</t><s>insert into chassis (id, car_id, material, color) values (1, 1, 'aluminum', 'silver') on conflict (id) do update set car_id = excluded.car_id, material = excluded.material, color = excluded.color</s>

CREATE TABLE engine(id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES car(id), type VARCHAR(50), hp INT)

CREATE TABLE chassis(id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES car(id), material VARCHAR(50), color VARCHAR(50))

CREATE TABLE maintenance(id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES car(id), type VARCHAR(50), date DATE)</t><s>INSERT INTO chassis (id, car_id, material, color) VALUES (1, 1, 'Aluminum', 'Silver') ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET car_id = excluded.car_id, material = excluded.material, color = excluded.color</s>

<t>CREATE TABLE maintenance(id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES car(id), type VARCHAR(50), date DATE)

CREATE TABLE engine(id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES car(id), type VARCHAR(50), hp INT)

CREATE TABLE tire(id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES car(id), brand VARCHAR(50), size VARCHAR(10), type VARCHAR(50))

CREATE TABLE chassis(id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES car(id), material VARCHAR(50), color VARCHAR(50))

CREATE TABLE car(id INT PRIMARY KEY, brand VARCHAR(50), model VARCHAR(50))</t><s>insert into chassis (id, car_id, material, color) values (1, 1, 'aluminum', 'silver') on conflict (id) do update set car_id = excluded.car_id, material = excluded.material, color = excluded.color</s>
